    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><a name="eolPage17" /><a name="FIS_UNIDENTIFIED_TABLE_9">Level 2 liabilities consist of
derivative liabilities (see Note 14).&#160;&#160;Under SFAS 157, the fair value
of the Company's derivative financial instruments is determined based on the
counterparties' valuation models that utilize market corroborated
inputs.&#160;&#160;The fair value of all derivative contracts is reflected on
the balance sheet.&#160;&#160;The current liability amounts represent the fair
values expected to be included in the results of operations for the subsequent
year.</a></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Level 3
assets consist of municipal bonds and floating rate preferred stock (see Note 3)
with an auction reset feature (&#8220;auction rate securities&#8221; or ARS).&#160;&#160;The
underlying assets for the municipal bonds are student loans which are
substantially backed by the federal government.&#160;&#160;Auction-rate
securities are long-term floating rate bonds or floating rate perpetual
preferred stock tied to short-term interest rates.&#160;&#160;After the initial
issuance of the securities, the interest rate on the securities is reset
periodically, at intervals established at the time of issuance (primarily every
twenty-eight days), based on market demand for a reset
period.&#160;&#160;Auction-rate securities are bought and sold in the
marketplace through a competitive bidding process often referred to as a &#8220;Dutch
auction&#8221;.&#160;&#160;If there is insufficient interest in the securities at the
time of an auction, the auction may not be completed and the rates may be reset
to predetermined &#8220;penalty&#8221; or &#8220;maximum&#8221; rates based on mathematical formulas in
accordance with each security's prospectus.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In
February 2008, auctions began to fail for these securities and each auction
since then has failed.&#160;&#160;Consequently, the investments are not
currently liquid.&#160;&#160;In the event the Company needed to access these
funds, they are not expected to be accessible until one of the following occurs:
a successful auction occurs, the issuer redeems the issue, a buyer is found
outside of the auction process or the underlying securities
mature.&#160;&#160;In October 2008, the Company received an offer (the &#8220;Offer&#8221;)
from UBS AG (&#8220;UBS&#8221;), one of its investment providers, to sell at par value
auction-rate securities originally purchased from UBS ($2,825,143) at anytime
during a two-year period beginning June 30, 2010.&#160;&#160;The Offer was
non-transferable and expired on November 14, 2008. On October 28, 2008 the
Company elected to participate in the Offer.&#160;&#160;&#160;The Company has
classified auction rate securities as short-term assets on our balance
sheet.&#160;&#160;In addition to the Offer, UBS is providing no net cost loans
up to 75% of the loan-to-market value of eligible auction rate securities until
June 30, 2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Typically,
the fair value of ARS investments approximates par value due to the frequent
resets through the auction process.&#160;&#160;While the Company continues to
earn interest on its ARS investments at the contractual rate, these investments
are not currently trading and therefore do not have a readily determinable
market value.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, the estimated fair value of the ARS no
longer approximates par value.&#160;&#160;At June 30, 2009, the Company&#8217;s
investment advisors provided a valuation based on Level 3 inputs for the ARS
investments.&#160;&#160;The investment advisors utilized a discounted cash flow
approach to arrive at this valuation. The assumptions used in preparing the
discounted cash flow model include estimates of, based on data available as of
June 30, 2009, interest rates, timing and amount of cash flows, credit and
liquidity premiums, and expected holding periods of the ARS.&#160;&#160;These
assumptions are volatile and subject to change as the underlying sources of
these assumptions and market conditions change.&#160;&#160;Based on
this</font></div><br>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">20</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
    </div><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Level 3
valuation, the Company valued the ARS investments at $2,574,935, which
represents a decline in value of $250,208 from par.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Although
there is uncertainty with regard to the short-term liquidity of these
securities, the Company continues to believe that the carrying value represents
the fair value of these marketable securities because of the overall quality of
the underlying investments and the anticipated future market for such
investments.&#160; In addition, the Company has the intent and ability to hold
these securities until the earlier of: the market for auction rate securities
stabilizes, the issuer refinances the underlying security, a buyer is found
outside of the auction process at acceptable terms, the underlying securities
have matured or the Company accepts the investment manager&#8217;s offer to redeem the
securities.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><a name="FORM10Q_05112009_HTM_EOLPAGE65" /><a name="FIS_UNIDENTIFIED_TABLE_36">Based on
the CIT financing, the expected positive operating cash flows, and the Company&#8217;s
ability to obtain no net cost loans up to 75% of the loan-to-market value, as
determined by UBS, on eligible auction rate securities, the Company does not
anticipate the current inability to liquidate the auction rate securities to
adversely affect the Company&#8217;s ability to conduct its business.
</a></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

for the assets measured at fair value using significant unobservable inputs
(Level 3):</font></div>

                </td>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">NOTE
13&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;FINANCIAL
INSTRUMENTS</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -9pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company&#8217;s non-derivative financial instruments include cash and cash
equivalents, accounts receivable, accounts payable and the line of credit. The
carrying amount of cash and cash equivalents, accounts receivable, accounts
payable, and the line of credit approximate fair value because of their
immediate or short-term maturities.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company&#8217;s accounts receivable relate to oil and natural gas sold to various
industry companies.&#160;&#160;Credit terms, typical of industry standards, are
of a short-term nature and the Company does not require
collateral.&#160;&#160;The Company&#8217;s accounts receivable at June 30, 2009 and
December&#160;31, 2008 do not represent significant credit risks as they are
dispersed across many counterparties.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">NOTE
14&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;DERIVATIVE
INSTRUMENTS AND PRICE RISK MANAGEMENT</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company utilizes commodity swap contracts to (i) reduce the effects of
volatility in price changes on the oil commodities it produces and sells, (ii)
reduce commodity price risk and (iii) provide a base level of cash
flow.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Crude
Oil Derivative Contracts Cash-flow Hedges</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company's designated cash-flow hedges under provisions of SFAS No. 133 consisted
of crude oil futures contracts.&#160; The contracts were used to establish floor
prices on anticipated future oil production. There were no net premiums received
or paid when the Company entered into these contracts.&#160;&#160;At settlement
any realized gains or losses are recorded as gain (loss) on derivatives, net, as
an increase or decrease in revenue on the statement of
operations.&#160;&#160;&#160;The Company realized a hedging loss of $125,878 and
a hedging gain of $1,300 for the six months ended June 30, 2009 and 2008,
respectively.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
following table reflects open commodity derivative contracts as of June 30,
2009, the associated volumes and the corresponding weighted average NYMEX
reference price.</font></div><br>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Overview
and Outlook</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We are an
oil and gas exploration and production company.&#160;&#160;Our properties are
located in Montana, North Dakota and New York.&#160;&#160;Our corporate strategy
is to build shareholder value through the development and acquisition of oil and
gas assets that exhibit economically producible hydrocarbons.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">During
the quarter ended June 30, 2009, we continued the development of our oil and gas
properties primarily in the Williston Basin Bakken play.&#160;&#160;We drilled,
completed or acquired interests in an additional 53 gross wells (approximately
1.87 net wells) during the quarter.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Slawson
Exploration Company Exploration and Development Agreement</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On May
22, 2009, we entered into an Exploration and Development Agreement with Slawson
Exploration Company, Inc. (&#8220;Slawson&#8221;) pursuant to which we acquired certain
North Dakota Bakken assets from Windsor Bakken LLC as part of a syndicate led by
privately owned Slawson.&#160;&#160;Pursuant to the Exploration and Development
Agreement, we purchased a five percent (5.0%) interest in oil and gas rights
covering approximately 60,000 undeveloped net acres.&#160;&#160;We also acquired
fourteen percent (14%) of the existing 59 gross Bakken and Three Forks producing
well bores in North Dakota including approximately 1,200 barrels of oil
production per day. In the</font></div><br>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">23</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
    </div><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">transaction
we purchased approximately 300,000 barrels of proven producing reserves as well
as approximately 3,000 net undeveloped acres for a total cost of
$7,300,000.&#160;&#160;The acreage includes several high-rate Parshall Field
wells that we believe offer significant infill drilling
potential.&#160;&#160;All consideration was paid in cash using additional
borrowing made available under our credit facility with CIT Capital USA Inc.
(&#8220;CIT&#8221;), as more fully described below.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Under the
Exploration and Development Agreement, we agreed to share pro-rata in the costs
associated with Slawson&#8217;s acquisition of the properties from Windsor Bakken LLC
and certain continuing obligations and commitments in connection with future
drilling activities on the subject properties.&#160;&#160;We may be subject to
forfeiture of certain portions of the properties in the event it does not elect
to participate in drilling wells on the properties, as fully described in the
Exploration and Development Agreement.&#160;&#160;Slawson will be responsible
for all operations concerning the properties, and is expected to drill up to 45
gross Bakken wells on the newly acquired acreage through 2010.&#160;&#160;We
currently expect drilling under the arrangement to be focused on approximately
23,000 acres in the core Bakken prospects located in Mountrail County,
encompassing a significant portion of our existing core Bakken
acreage.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2009
Drilling Projects</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We are
engaged in numerous drilling activities on properties presently owned and intend
to drill or develop other properties acquired in the future.&#160;&#160;We
drilled or acquired interests in an additional 53 gross wells (approximately
1.87 net wells) during the quarter.&#160;&#160;In 2009, we intend to continue
drilling efforts on our existing acreage in North Dakota and Montana, and to
commence drilling or participate in approximately 60-70 new gross wells
including first and second quarter completions.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As of
June 30, 2009, we have a total of 140 gross wells that are either drilling,
completing or producing, including 104 producing wells and 36 drilling or
completing wells.&#160;&#160;Permits continue to be issued for drilling units in
which we have acreage interests within North Dakota and Montana.&#160;&#160;We
do not know if or when applicable operators will chose to commence drilling
activities for any contemplated well that is not yet drilling.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Production
History</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
following table presents information about our produced oil and gas volumes
during the three month and six month periods ended June 30, 2009 compared to the
three month and six month periods ended June 30, 2008.&#160;&#160;As of June 30,
2009, we were selling oil and natural gas from a total of 104 gross wells
(approximately 4.97 net wells), compared to 9 gross wells (approximately .92 net
wells) at June 30, 2008.&#160;&#160;All data presented below is derived from
accrued revenue and production volumes for the relevant period
indicated.</font></div>

              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">0.93</font></div>
            </td>
          </tr>
      </table>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Results
of Operations for the periods ended June 30, 2008 and June 30,
2009.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our first
well commenced drilling in the fourth quarter of 2007.&#160;&#160;During 2008 we
significantly increased our drilling activities, generated income and achieved
net earnings in the third and fourth quarters of 2008 and for the 2008 fiscal
year as a whole.&#160;&#160;Our current business activities are focused
primarily on developing our current</font></div><br>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">25</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
    </div><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">acreage
position and identifying potential strategic acreage and production acquisitions
to continue to consistently increase production and revenues.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">During
the quarter ended June 30, 2009, we continued the development of our oil and gas
properties primarily in the Williston Basin Bakken play.&#160;&#160;As of June
30, 2009,&#160;we had established production from 104 total gross wells in which
we hold working interests, only nine of which had established production as of
June 30, 2008.&#160;&#160;Our production at June 30, 2009 approximated 967
barrels of oil per day, compared to approximately 792 barrels of oil per day at
March 31, 2009.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We
drilled with a 100% success rate in the quarter ended June 30,
2009.&#160;&#160;We have 101 Bakken or Three Forks wells completed and three
successful Red River discoveries at June 30, 2009.&#160;&#160;As of June 30,
2009, we expect to participate in the drilling of approximately 60-70 gross oil
wells (six to seven net) in 2009.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We
recognized $2,418,496 in revenues from sales of oil and natural gas for the
three months ended June 30, 2009, compared to $764,528 for the three months
ended June 30, 2008.&#160;&#160;We recognized $3,059,230 in revenues from sales
of oil and natural gas for the six months ended June 30, 2009, compared to
$1,050,257 for the six months ended June 30, 2008.&#160;&#160;These increases in
revenue are due primarily to our continued addition of wells period-over-period
and our realization of production from such wells.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Total
expenses for the three-month period ended June 30, 2008, were $576,487 and for
the three-month period ended June 30, 2009, were $1,608,937.&#160;&#160;We had
net income of $283,465 for the three-month period ended June 30, 2008, and net
income of $315,924 (representing approximately $0.01per share) for the
three-month period ended June 30, 2009.&#160;&#160;Total expenses for the
six-month period ended June 30, 2008, were $1,147,062 and for the six-month
period ended June 30, 2009, were $2,735,983.&#160;&#160;We had net income of
$96,188 for the six-month period ended June 30, 2008, and net income of $8,599
(representing approximately $0.00 per share) for the six-month period ended June
30, 2009.&#160;&#160;These increases in expenses are due primarily to increased
production expenses, severance taxes and depletion expenses associated with our
continued addition of oil and gas production.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Liquidity
and Capital Resources</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We have
historically met our capital requirements through the issuance of common stock
and by borrowings.&#160;&#160;We believe we improved our available liquidity in
the quarter ended June 30, 2009 compared to the prior fiscal quarter through
amending our credit facility with CIT and raising additional equity capital
through a registered direct offering of our common stock, as more fully
described below.&#160;&#160;In the future, we anticipate we will be able to
provide the necessary liquidity by the revenues generated from the sales of our
oil and gas reserves in our existing properties, however, if we do not generate
sufficient sales revenues we will continue to finance our operations through
equity and/or debt financings.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
following table summarizes total current assets, total current liabilities and
working capital at June 30, 2009.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Current
Assets&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;$&#160;&#160;&#160;21,876,015</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Current

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Working
Capital&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
$&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;5,853,685</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">CIT
Capital USA, Inc. Credit Facility</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>On February 27, 2009, we completed the
closing of a revolving credit facility with CIT that will provide up to a
maximum principal amount of $25 million of working capital for exploration and
production operations.&#160;&#160;The borrowing base of funds available under
the facility will be redetermined semi-annually based upon the net present
value, discounted at 10% per annum, of the future net revenues expected to
accrue from our interests in proved reserves estimated to be produced from our
oil and gas properties.&#160;&#160;The facility terminates on February 27,
2012.</font></div><br>

      <div id="FTR">

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 18.7pt"></font>The facility initially provided an
$11 million borrowing base.&#160;&#160;On May 22, 2009, we amended the facility
to increase the available borrowing base to $16 million.&#160;&#160;The
amendment was executed in connection with our purchase of certain leasehold
interests from Slawson pursuant to the Exploration and Development Agreement
described above.&#160;&#160;We may use the additional funds available as a
result of the amendment solely to fund the acquisition of properties from
Slawson and other associated costs, expenses and fees, unless otherwise agreed
to by CIT.&#160;&#160;Following the amendment, an additional $9 million of
financing could become available upon subsequent borrowing base redeterminations
based on the deployment of funds from the facility.&#160;&#160;We expect to
redetermine our borrowing base as of June 30, 2009.&#160;&#160;Given recent
production growth and increases in commodity prices, we believe it is likely the
borrowing base available under the facility may be further increased at that
time.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">All of
our obligations under the facility and the swap agreements with Macquarie
continue to be secured by a first priority security interest in any and all of
our assets pursuant to the terms of a Guaranty and Collateral Agreement and
perfected by a mortgage, notice of pledge and security and similar
documents.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">$13.5
Million Registered Direct Offering</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>On June 29, 2009 we completed a
registered direct offering of 2,250,000 shares of our common stock at $6.00 per
share, resulting in gross proceeds of approximately
$13.5&#160;million.&#160;&#160;The offering was conducted pursuant to Northern
Oil&#8217;s effective shelf registration statement previously filed with the
SEC.&#160;&#160;&#160;Subsequent to June 30, 2009 we&#160;&#160;used most of the
net proceeds from the offering to repay a portion of the current borrowings
under our credit facility with CIT, primarily including borrowings incurred in
connection with our May 2009 acquisition of additional Bakken
assets.&#160;&#160;&#160;We paid fees and commissions of $798,951 in the
transaction.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Satisfaction
of Our Cash Obligations for the Next 12 Months</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">With the
amendment of the CIT credit facility and the addition of equity capital in the
quarter ended June 30, 2009, we believe we will be funded to meet our drilling
commitments and expected general and administrative expenses for the next twelve
months.&#160;&#160;Nonetheless, any strategic acquisition of assets may require
us to access the capital markets again at some point in the next 12
months.&#160;&#160;We believe there may be distressed situations that will arise
in 2009 that may make the acquisition of assets a viable strategy, and we will
evaluate any potential opportunities as they arise.&#160;&#160;Given our
non-leveraged asset base and anticipated growing cash flows, we believe we are
in a position to take advantage of any distressed opportunities that may
arise.&#160;&#160;However, there can be no assurance that any additional capital
will be available to us on favorable terms or at all.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Over the
next 24 months it is possible that our existing capital, the CIT facility and
anticipated funds from operations may not be sufficient to sustain continued
development of our current acreage position.&#160;&#160;Consequently, we may
seek additional capital in the future to fund growth and expansion through
additional equity or debt financing or credit facilities.&#160;&#160;No
assurance can be made that such financing would be available, and if available
it may take either the form of debt or equity.&#160;&#160;In either case, the
financing could have a negative impact on our financial condition and our
stockholders.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Though we
achieved profitability in 2008, our prospects must be considered in light of the
risks, expenses and difficulties frequently encountered by companies in their
early stage of operations, particularly companies in the oil and gas exploration
industry.&#160;&#160;Such risks include, but are not limited to, an evolving and
unpredictable business model and the management of growth.&#160;&#160;To address
these risks we must, among other things, implement and successfully execute our
business and marketing strategy, continue to develop and upgrade technology and
products, respond to competitive developments, and attract, retain and motivate
qualified personnel.&#160;&#160;There can be no assurance that we will be
successful in addressing such risks, and the failure to do so can have a
material adverse effect on our business prospects, financial condition and
results of operations.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Contractual
Obligations and Commitments</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As of
June 30, 2009, we did not have any material long-term debt obligations other
than the CIT credit facility and subordinated notes issued to our chief
executive and chief financial officers&#160;&#160;in the aggregate principle
amount of $500,000.&#160;&#160;We also did not have any material capital lease
obligations, operating lease obligations or purchase obligations requiring
future payments except our office lease that expires on January 31, 2013,
and</font></div><br>

3.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Quantitative and
Qualitative Disclosures about Market Risk</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our
quantitative and qualitative disclosures about market risk for changes in
commodity prices and interest rates are included in Item 7A of our Annual Report
on Form&#160;10-K for the fiscal year ended December 31, 2008 and have not
materially changed since that report was filed.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Hedging
Activities</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our
credit facility with CIT requires that we enter into a swap agreement with
Macquarie Bank Limited (&#8220;Macquarie&#8221;) to hedge certain quantities of oil
production over the 36-month term of the facility.&#160;&#160;In general, we do
not expect to use hedges beyond the extent required by our
lenders.&#160;&#160;As of June 30, 2009, our current hedging consisted
exclusively of WTI-NYMEX crude oil swap agreements settled
monthly.&#160;&#160;We originally entered into certain swap agreements when we
initiated the facility on February 27, 2009 and entered into additional swap
agreements when we amended our facility on May 22, 2009.&#160;&#160;All of our
swap arrangements are settled based upon a constant price per barrel of oil
represented by the swap contract.</font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">A

$28,200 unrealized gain (loss)&#160;on hedging activities as of June 30,
2009.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Interest Rate
Risk</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our
credit facility with CIT subjects us to interest rate risk on borrowings under
that facility.&#160;&#160;Our facility allows us to fix the interest rate of
borrowings under the facility for all or a portion of the principal balance for
a period up to six months.&#160;&#160;To the extent the interest rate is fixed,
interest rate changes affect the instrument&#8217;s fair market value but do not
impact results of operations or cash flows.&#160;&#160;Conversely, for the
portion of our borrowings that has a floating interest rate, interest rate
changes will not affect the fair market value but will impact future results of
operations and cash flows.</font></div><br>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Item
4. Controls and Procedures.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Evaluation
of Disclosure Controls and Procedures</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We
maintain a system of disclosure controls and procedures that is designed to
ensure that information required to be disclosed in our Exchange Act reports is
recorded, processed, summarized and reported within the time periods specified
in rules and forms of the SEC, and that such information is accumulated and
communicated to our management, including our Chief Executive Officer and Chief
Financial Officer, as appropriate, to allow timely decisions regarding required
disclosures.</font></div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As of
June 30, 2009, our management, including our Chief Executive Officer and Chief
Financial Officer, had evaluated the effectiveness of the design and operation
of our disclosure controls and procedures (as defined in Exchange Act
Rules&#160;13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e)) pursuant to Rule&#160;13a-15(b) under the
Exchange Act.&#160;&#160;Based upon and as of the date of the evaluation, our
Chief Executive Officer and Chief Financial Officer concluded that information
required to be disclosed is recorded, processed, summarized and reported within
the specified periods and is accumulated and communicated to management,
including our Chief Executive Officer and Chief Financial Officer, to allow for
timely decisions regarding required disclosure of material information required
to be included in our periodic SEC reports.&#160;&#160;Based on the foregoing,
our management determined that our disclosure controls and procedures were
effective as of June 30, 2009.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Changes
in Internal Control over Financial Reporting</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">There
were no changes in our internal control over financial reporting that occurred
during the three months ended June 30, 2009, that materially affected or are
reasonably likely to materially affect our internal control over financial
reporting.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">PART
II - OTHER INFORMATION</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Item
1.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Legal
Proceedings.</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our
company is subject to litigation claims and governmental and regulatory
proceedings arising in the ordinary course of business.&#160;&#160;No material
developments have occurred in any pending litigation matters subsequent to the
filing of our Annual Report on Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended December 31,
2008.&#160;&#160;Our management believes that all litigation matters in which we
are involved are not likely to have a material adverse effect on our financial
position, cash flows or results of operations.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div>
      <table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%">
          <tr valign="top">
            <td style="WIDTH: 72pt">
              <div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
      </font></div>
            </td>
            <td>
              <div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Item
      1A.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">Risk
      Factors</font>.</font></div>
            </td>
          </tr>
      </table>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Other
than with respect to the addition of one risk factor and the restatement of
another risk factor, each as described below, there have been no material
changes to the risk factors disclosed in the &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; section of our
Annual Report on Form 10-K for the year ended December 31, 2008.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We add
the following additional risk factor:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As
a non-operator, our development of successful operations relies extensively on
third-parties who, if not successful, could have a material adverse affect on
our results of operation.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We have
only participated in wells operated by third-parties. Our current ability to
develop successful business operations depends on the success of our consultants
and drilling partners. As a result, we do not control the timing or success of
the development, exploitation, production and exploration activities relating to
our leasehold interests. If our consultants and drilling partners are not
successful in such activities relating to our leasehold interests, or are unable
or unwilling to perform, our financial condition and results of operation may be
materially adversely affected.</font></div><br>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">29</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; COLOR: #000000; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;
</font></div>
      </div>
    </div><br>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Our
current risk factor captioned <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">&#8220;Estimates of oil and natural gas
reserves that we make may be inaccurate and our actual revenues may be lower
than our financial projections&#8221;</font> is restated as follows:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Estimates of oil
and natural gas reserves that we make may be inaccurate and our actual revenues
may be lower than our financial
projections.</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;We
will make estimates of oil and natural gas reserves, upon which we will base our
financial projections. We will make these reserve estimates using various
assumptions, including assumptions as to oil and natural gas prices, drilling
and operating expenses, capital expenditures, taxes and availability of funds.
Some of these assumptions are inherently subjective, and the accuracy of our
reserve estimates relies in part on the ability of our management team,
engineers and other advisors to make accurate assumptions. Economic factors
beyond our control, such as interest rates, will also impact the value of our
reserves.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Determining
the amount of oil and gas recoverable from various formations where we have
exploration and production activities involves great uncertainty. For example,
in 2006, the North Dakota Industrial Commission published an article that
identified three different estimates of generated oil recoverable from the
Bakken formation. An organic chemist estimated 50% of the reserves in the Bakken
formation to be technically recoverable, an oil company estimated a recovery
factor of 18%, and values presented in the North Dakota Industrial Commission
Oil and Gas Hearings ranged from 3 to 10%.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The
process of estimating oil and natural gas reserves is complex and will require
us to use significant decisions and assumptions in the evaluation of available
geological, geophysical, engineering and economic data for each property. As a
result, our reserve estimates will be inherently imprecise. Actual future
production, oil and natural gas prices, revenues, taxes, development
expenditures, operating expenses and quantities of recoverable oil and natural
gas reserves may vary substantially from those we estimate. If actual production
results vary substantially from our reserve estimates, this could materially
reduce our revenues and result in the impairment of our oil and natural gas
interests.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Item
4.&#160;&#160;Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;We
held our Annual Meeting of Shareholders on June 18, 2009.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

            <td>
              <div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Disclosed
      in this report any change in the registrant&#8217;s internal control over
      financial reporting that occurred during the registrant&#8217;s most recent
      fiscal quarter (the registrant&#8217;s fourth fiscal quarter in the case of an
      annual report) that has materially affected, or is reasonably likely to
      materially affect, the registrant&#8217;s internal control over financial
      reporting; and</font></div>
            </td>
          </tr>
